You're Welcome to Try (You Wouldn't Be the First One to Fail)

by Lexus (Beautiful_Ruin)

Summary

Agatha and Rio are teachers at the same school. It's Rio's first year there, and she doesn't appreciate the way Agatha treats people. She makes a comment about teaching Agatha some manners when she thinks Agatha's left the room, and Agatha overhears, issuing her own challenge. "You're welcome to try."

Written for day 3 of AgatharioKink: brat/brat tamer

but it will be a multi-chap

The words and the voice belong to Agatha Harkness, one of the special ed teachers. Rio has never had a confrontation with her directly – Agatha doesn’t usually use the staff break room and their classrooms are on opposite sides of the building – but she’s heard enough insults thrown around to know who’s speaking.

“Just go around him,” someone else says.

Rio’s secondhand embarrassment flares hot and she’s humiliated on Agatha’s behalf.

Fortunately, Agatha leaves the break room as soon as her mug is full.

Nobody even says anything about it, they all just act like nothing happened and go back to whatever they were doing. Well, fine. If they don’t want to stand up for themselves, Rio isn’t going to do it for them. She likes her job.

She does idly wonder why Agatha suddenly needed coffee from the staff break room, though. It’s the first time all year she’s seen that happen. Maybe the bitch got banned from every coffee shop in a ten-mile radius.

That thought makes Rio intensely amused. She tries not to think about how satisfying it would be to slap Agatha Harkness across the face. That road would only lead to her own ruin, she’s sure.
